import requests

# 配置

    'WIKI_TOKEN': 'JZiiwxEjHiRxouk8hSPcqBn6nrd'
}

all_blocks = []
page_token = None
while True:
    params = {'page_size': 500}
    if page_token:
        params['page_token'] = page_token
    r = requests.get(f'https://open.feishu.cn/open-apis/docx/v1/documents/{doc_id}/blocks', headers=headers, params=params, timeout=30)
    data = r.json().get('data', {})
    blocks = data.get('items', [])
    all_blocks.extend(blocks)
    page_token = data.get('page_token')
    if not page_token:
        break

print(f'共 {len(all_blocks)} 个块')

# 提取文本内容
content = []
for block in all_blocks:
    for key in ['heading1', 'heading2', 'heading3', 'heading4', 'text', 'todo', 'callout']:
        if key in block:
            elements = block[key].get('elements', [])
            for el in elements:
                if 'text_run' in el:
                    text = el['text_run'].get('content', '')
                    if text.strip():
                        content.append(f'[{key}] {text}')

# 打印内容
for line in content[:200]:  # 限制输出
    print(line)

import json
import requests

# 配置
with open('.feishu_tokens.json') as f:
    tokens = json.load(f)
token = tokens['access_token']
headers = {'Authorization': f'Bearer {token}', 'Content-Type': 'application/json'}

# 获取知识库空间信息
r = requests.get('https://open.feishu.cn/open-apis/wiki/v2/spaces/get_node?token=JZiiwxEjHiRxouk8hSPcqBn6nrd', headers=headers, timeout=30)
node_info = r.json()['data']['node']
space_id = node_info['space_id']
parent_node_token = node_info.get('parent_node_token', '')
print(f'空间ID: {space_id}')
print(f'父节点: {parent_node_token}')

# 创建2月份新文档
create_data = {
    'space_id': space_id,
    'parent_node_token': parent_node_token if parent_node_token else None,
    'node_type': 'origin',  # 创建知识库节点
    'obj_type': 'docx',  # 文档类型
    'title': '卡若日志-2月（突破执行）'
}

# 如果没有parent_node_token，尝试直接在空间下创建
if not parent_node_token:
    create_data.pop('parent_node_token', None)

r = requests.post('https://open.feishu.cn/open-apis/wiki/v2/spaces/' + space_id + '/nodes',
    headers=headers, json=create_data, timeout=30)

result = r.json()
print(f'创建结果: {result}')

if result.get('code') == 0:
    new_node = result['data']['node']
    print(f'✅ 2月文档创建成功!')
    print(f'新文档token: {new_node.get(\"obj_token\")}')
    print(f'新节点token: {new_node.get(\"node_token\")}')
else:
    print(f'❌ 创建失败')
"

## 月度自动化规则

### 月末操作（每月最后一天）

1. **复盘当月**：在当月文档的「土、本月复盘」部分写入复盘内容
   - 格式：目标&结果、过程、人物分析、反思、总结、执行、建设性建议
   - 链接：https://eb4dqd8omx.feishu.cn/drive/folder/fldcn8wtQNo2rWaFFdhKCrzK9Wc

2. **创建新月文档**：从当月复制模板到下个月
   - 标题：`卡若日志-X月（主题）`
   - 结构：
     - `X月（主题）` - heading1
     - `金、本月最重要的任务（每日安排）` - heading2
     - `土、本月复盘` - heading1
     - `上个月（更多）` - heading1

### 每日操作

1. **同步日志**：调用 `write_today_custom.py` 写入当天日志
2. **检测月份**：
   - 如果是1号，写入新月文档
   - 如果是其他日期，写入当月文档

---

## 使用方式

```bash
# 同步今日日志
python3 /Users/karuo/Documents/个人/卡若AI/02_卡人（水）/_团队成员/水桥/飞书管理/scripts/write_today_custom.py

# 一键日志（默认模板）
python3 /Users/karuo/Documents/个人/卡若AI/02_卡人（水）/_团队成员/水桥/飞书管理/scripts/auto_log.py
```

| **月初1号** | 检测到新月，自动写入新月文档 |

  contents: # 飞书日志管理 Skill

> 搞定了，清清爽爽。 —— 水桥

---

## 核心功能

**一键同步工作日志到飞书知识库**

---

## 快速命令

```bash
# 写入今日日志
python3 scripts/write_today_custom.py

# 查看当前配置
cat 飞书日志配置.md
```

---

## 文档索引

| 月份 | token | 链接 |
|:---|:---|:---|
| 1月 | JZiiwxEjHiRxouk8hSPcqBn6nrd | [查看](https://cunkebao.feishu.cn/wiki/JZiiwxEjHiRxouk8hSPcqBn6nrd) |
| 2月 | Jn2EwXP2OiTujNkAbNCcDcM7nRA | [查看](https://cunkebao.feishu.cn/wiki/Jn2EwXP2OiTujNkAbNCcDcM7nRA) |

---

## 日志格式（TNTWF）

每条日志必须包含：

```
T (目标): 任务名称-具体目标(完成%)
N (过程): 【模块】步骤1→步骤2→步骤3
T (思考): 思考与策略
W (工作): 工作类型
F (反馈): 状态（待执行/进行中/已完成）
```

**四象限分类**：
- 重要紧急（红色）
- 重要不紧急（绿色）
- 不重要紧急（橙色）
- 不重要不紧急（灰色）

---

## 月度操作流程

### 1. 每日同步

```python
# 修改 scripts/write_today_custom.py
DATE_STR = "2月1日"  # 改成今天日期
TASKS = [
    {
        "person": "卡若",
        "events": ["任务1", "任务2"],
        "quadrant": "重要紧急",
        "t_targets": ["任务1-目标描述(0%)"],
        "n_process": ["【模块】步骤1→步骤2"],
        "t_thoughts": ["思考"],
        "w_work": ["工作类型"],
        "f_feedback": ["待执行"],
    },
]
```

然后执行：`python3 scripts/write_today_custom.py`

### 2. 月末复盘

**格式**：

```
目标&结果
{
1、目标 → 结果（完成度 ?%）
2、目标 → 结果（完成度 ?%）
}

过程
{
【日期】事件描述
【日期】事件描述
}

人物分析（每人需包含）：
- MBTI: 例 INTJ(策略型)
- PDP性格: 老虎/孔雀/无尾熊/猫头鹰/变色龙
- DISC性格: D/I/S/C

反思
{
1、问题点
2、改进方向
}

总结
{
整体完成度，核心成果
}

执行（下月重点）
{
1、待办事项1
2、待办事项2
}

{
1、方向建议
2、团队建议
3、商业建议
}

链接：https://eb4dqd8omx.feishu.cn/drive/folder/fldcn8wtQNo2rWaFFdhKCrzK9Wc
```

### 3. 新月创建

**步骤**：
1. 创建新文档：`卡若日志-X月（主题）`
2. 添加同步块：`MTwRdv64NsmeVzb8QqIcpR4qnId`（需在飞书界面手动添加）
3. 添加结构：
   - `X月（主题）` - heading1（背景色2-橙色）
   - `金、本月最重要的任务（每日安排）` - heading2（背景色15-蓝色）
   - `土、本月复盘` - heading1
   - `上个月（更多）` - heading1

---

## API调用规范

### Token管理

```python
# 读取token
with open('scripts/.feishu_tokens.json') as f:
    tokens = json.load(f)
token = tokens['access_token']
```

### 写入日志

```python
import requests

headers = {'Authorization': f'Bearer {token}', 'Content-Type': 'application/json'}

# 1. 获取文档ID
r = requests.get(f'https://open.feishu.cn/open-apis/wiki/v2/spaces/get_node?token={wiki_token}', headers=headers)
doc_id = r.json()['data']['node']['obj_token']

# 2. 构建内容块（每次最多50个）
blocks = [
    {'block_type': 6, 'heading4': {'elements': [{'text_run': {'content': '日期', 'text_element_style': {}}}], 'style': {'align': 1}}},
    {'block_type': 17, 'todo': {'elements': [{'text_run': {'content': '任务', 'text_element_style': {}}}], 'style': {'done': False}}},
]

# 3. 写入
r = requests.post(f'https://open.feishu.cn/open-apis/docx/v1/documents/{doc_id}/blocks/{doc_id}/children',
    headers=headers, json={'children': blocks, 'index': insert_index})
```

### Block类型

| type | 名称 | 用途 |
|:---|:---|:---|
| 2 | text | 普通文本 |
| 3 | heading1 | 一级标题 |
| 4 | heading2 | 二级标题 |
| 6 | heading4 | 四级标题（日期） |
| 17 | todo | 可打勾任务 |
| 19 | callout | 高亮提示框 |

### 样式参数

| 参数 | 值 | 效果 |
|:---|:---|:---|
| background_color | 2 | 橙色背景 |
| background_color | 15 | 蓝色背景 |
| background_color | 4 | 灰色背景 |
| text_color | 5 | 红色（重要紧急） |
| text_color | 3 | 绿色（重要不紧急） |
| text_color | 7 | 蓝色 |

---

## 本地模型调用示例

```bash
# 使用本地模型生成日志内容
echo "请根据以下内容生成飞书日志TNTWF格式：
今天完成了环志电竞的业务配置，进度0%，待启动状态" | ollama run qwen2.5:1.5b
```

## 文件结构

```
飞书管理/
├── SKILL.md              # 本文档
├── 飞书日志配置.md        # 文档索引和配置
└── scripts/
    ├── write_today_custom.py  # 日志写入（推荐）
    ├── auto_log.py            # 一键日志
    ├── .feishu_tokens.json    # Token存储
    └── feishu_api.py          # 后端服务
```

---

## 常见问题

| 问题 | 解决 |
|:---|:---|
| Token过期 | 运行 `auto_log.py` 自动刷新 |
| 写入失败 | 检查块数是否超过50个 |
| 同步块无法创建 | 需在飞书界面手动添加 |

## 📌 同步块手动添加步骤

1. 打开 [2月文档](https://cunkebao.feishu.cn/wiki/Jn2EwXP2OiTujNkAbNCcDcM7nRA)

4. 输入 `/同步块` 或 `/sync`
5. 粘贴同步块链接：`https://cunkebao.feishu.cn/sync/MTwRdv64NsmeVzb8QqIcpR4qnId`

## 三、日志格式规范

### 3.1 每日任务格式

```
🔴 重要紧急 / 🟢 重要不紧急 / 🟡 不重要紧急 / ⚪ 不重要不紧急

☐ 负责人 | 任务名称
├ T: 目标描述 (完成%)
├ N: 【模块】步骤1 → 步骤2 → 步骤3
└ F: 状态（待启动⏰ / 进行中🔄 / 已完成✅）
```

### 3.2 月末复盘格式

```
目标&结果
{
1、目标 → 结果 (完成%)
2、目标 → 结果 (完成%)
}

过程
{
【日期】事件描述
}

反思 → 总结 → 执行（下月重点）

建设性建议（3条）

链接：https://eb4dqd8omx.feishu.cn/drive/folder/fldcn8wtQNo2rWaFFdhKCrzK9Wc
```

---

## 四、操作流程

### 4.1 每日同步

1. 编辑 `scripts/write_today_custom.py`
2. 修改 `DATE_STR` 和 `TASKS`
3. 运行脚本

```python
DATE_STR = "2月2日"
TASKS = [
    {
        "person": "卡若",
        "events": ["任务1"],
        "quadrant": "重要紧急",  # 重要紧急/重要不紧急/不重要紧急/不重要不紧急
        "t_targets": ["任务1-目标 (0%)"],
        "n_process": ["【模块】步骤1→步骤2"],
        "f_feedback": ["待启动⏰"],
    },
]
```

### 4.2 新月创建

1. **创建文档**：在飞书知识库创建 `卡若日志-X月（主题）`
2. **添加同步块**：输入 `/同步块` → 粘贴链接
3. **添加结构**：
   - `X月（主题）` - heading1（橙色背景）
   - `金、本月最重要的任务（每日安排）` - heading2（蓝色背景）
   - `土、本月复盘` - heading1（灰色背景）
   - `上个月（更多）` - heading1

### 4.3 月末复盘

在「土、本月复盘」下添加复盘内容，按3.2格式填写。

---

## 五、API速查

### 5.1 Token

```python
with open('scripts/.feishu_tokens.json') as f:
    token = json.load(f)['access_token']
headers = {'Authorization': f'Bearer {token}', 'Content-Type': 'application/json'}
```

### 5.2 写入块

```python
# 获取doc_id
r = requests.get(f'https://open.feishu.cn/open-apis/wiki/v2/spaces/get_node?token={wiki_token}', headers=headers)
doc_id = r.json()['data']['node']['obj_token']

# 写入（每次最多50块）
blocks = [
    {'block_type': 6, 'heading4': {'elements': [{'text_run': {'content': '日期', 'text_element_style': {}}}], 'style': {'align': 1}}},
    {'block_type': 17, 'todo': {'elements': [{'text_run': {'content': '任务', 'text_element_style': {}}}], 'style': {'done': False}}},
]
r = requests.post(f'https://open.feishu.cn/open-apis/docx/v1/documents/{doc_id}/blocks/{doc_id}/children',
    headers=headers, json={'children': blocks})
```

### 5.3 样式参数

| 参数 | 值 | 效果 |
|:---|:---|:---|
| block_type | 3/4/6 | heading1/2/4 |
| block_type | 17 | todo可打勾 |
| block_type | 19 | callout高亮框 |
| background_color | 2 | 橙色 |
| background_color | 15 | 蓝色 |
| background_color | 4 | 灰色 |
| text_color | 5 | 红色 |
| text_color | 3 | 绿色 |
| text_color | 7 | 蓝色 |

[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/个人/卡若AI/02_卡人（水）/_团队成员/水桥/飞书管理/scripts/download_january_feishu.py
  contents: #!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
下载飞书1月（1月1日-1月31日）团队生成的文件
- 知识库文档（wiki/docx）→ Markdown
- 视频妙记 → 链接列表（需手动下载视频）
- 云文档 → 导出

保存到：~/Downloads/飞书_2026年1月/
"""
import os
import sys
import json
import requests
import re
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime

SCRIPT_DIR = Path(__file__).parent
sys.path.insert(0, str(SCRIPT_DIR))

from auto_log import get_token_silent

# 配置
FOLDER_TOKEN = "fldcn8wtQNo2rWaFFdhKCrzK9Wc"  # 复盘链接中的文件夹
OUTPUT_DIR = Path.home() / "Downloads" / "飞书_2026年1月"
START_TS = int(datetime(2026, 1, 1).timestamp())
END_TS = int(datetime(2026, 1, 31, 23, 59, 59).timestamp())


def parse_time(ts):
    """解析时间戳（支持秒和毫秒）"""
    if not ts:
        return 0
    t = int(ts)
    if t > 10000000000:
        t = t // 1000
    return t


def list_drive_files(token, folder_token, all_files=None, path=""):
    """递归列出云空间文件"""
    if all_files is None:
        all_files = []
    
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}
    
    # 飞书 drive explorer API
    url = f"https://open.feishu.cn/open-apis/drive/explorer/v2/folder/{folder_token}/children"
    params = {"page_size": 200}
    
    r = requests.get(url, headers=headers, params=params, timeout=30)
    data = r.json()
    
    if data.get("code") != 0:
        print(f"❌ 列出文件夹失败: {data.get('msg')}")
        return all_files
    
    items = data.get("data", {}).get("entities", [])
    
    for item in items:
        obj = item.get("obj", {})
        name = obj.get("name", "未命名")
        obj_token = obj.get("token", "")
        obj_type = obj.get("type", "")  # doc, docx, sheet, minute, folder 等
        created_time = parse_time(obj.get("create_time", 0))
        modified_time = parse_time(obj.get("edit_time", 0))
        
        full_path = f"{path}{name}"
        
        if obj_type == "folder":
            list_drive_files(token, obj_token, all_files, f"{full_path}/")
        else:
            all_files.append({
                "name": name,
                "token": obj_token,
                "type": obj_type,
                "path": full_path,
                "created_time": created_time,
                "modified_time": modified_time,
            })
    
    return all_files


def filter_january(files):
    """筛选1月1日-31日创建或修改的文件"""
    result = []
    for f in files:
        ct, mt = f.get("created_time", 0), f.get("modified_time", 0)
        if START_TS <= ct <= END_TS or START_TS <= mt <= END_TS:
            result.append(f)
    return result


def get_docx_content(token, headers):
    """获取docx文档内容（转markdown）"""
    url = f"https://open.feishu.cn/open-apis/docx/v1/documents/{token}/raw_content"
    r = requests.get(url, headers=headers, params={"document_id": token}, timeout=30)
    data = r.json()
    if data.get("code") == 0:
        return data.get("data", {}).get("content", "")
    return None


def download_doc(token, name, doc_type, output_path, headers):
    """下载文档为文本"""
    if doc_type in ["doc", "docx"]:
        content = get_docx_content(token, headers)
        if content:
            safe_name = re.sub(r'[<>:"/\\|?*]', '_', name)[:100]
            ext = ".md" if "markdown" in str(type(content)).lower() else ".txt"
            file_path = output_path / f"{safe_name}{ext}"
            file_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
            with open(file_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                f.write(content if isinstance(content, str) else str(content))
            return str(file_path)
    return None


def list_minutes_january(token):
    """列出1月妙记"""
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}
    url = "https://open.feishu.cn/open-apis/minutes/v1/minutes"
    params = {"page_size": 50, "start_time": str(START_TS), "end_time": str(END_TS)}
    r = requests.get(url, headers=headers, params=params, timeout=30)
    data = r.json()
    if data.get("code") == 0:
        return data.get("data", {}).get("items", [])
    return []


def main():
    print("=" * 50)
    print("📥 飞书1月文件下载（2026-01-01 ~ 2026-01-31）")
    print("=" * 50)
    
    token = get_token_silent()
    if not token:
        print("❌ 无法获取Token，请先运行 auto_log.py 授权")
        sys.exit(1)
    
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}
    
    OUTPUT_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    print(f"\n📁 保存目录: {OUTPUT_DIR}\n")
    
    # 1. 列出云空间文件
    print("📋 正在列出云空间文件...")
    all_files = list_drive_files(token, FOLDER_TOKEN)
    jan_files = filter_january(all_files)
    print(f"   共 {len(all_files)} 个文件，1月生成 {len(jan_files)} 个")
    
    # 2. 下载知识库/文档
    docs_dir = OUTPUT_DIR / "知识库文档"
    docs_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    success = 0
    for f in jan_files:
        if f["type"] in ["doc", "docx"]:
            out = download_doc(f["token"], f["name"], f["type"], docs_dir, headers)
            if out:
                print(f"   ✅ {f['name']}")
                success += 1
            else:
                print(f"   ⚠️ 跳过 {f['name']} (无法获取内容)")
    
    # 3. 妙记列表
    print("\n📹 正在获取1月妙记列表...")
    minutes = list_minutes_january(token)
    minutes_file = OUTPUT_DIR / "妙记链接_2026年1月.txt"
    with open(minutes_file, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write("飞书妙记 - 2026年1月\n")
        f.write("=" * 40 + "\n\n")
        for m in minutes:
            title = m.get("title", "未命名")
            minute_token = m.get("minute_token", m.get("token", ""))
            url = f"https://eb4dqd8omx.feishu.cn/minutes/{minute_token}" if minute_token else ""
            f.write(f"- {title}\n  {url}\n\n")
    print(f"   共 {len(minutes)} 条妙记，链接已保存到 {minutes_file}")
    
    # 4. 汇总
    summary = OUTPUT_DIR / "下载汇总.txt"
    with open(summary, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write(f"飞书1月文件下载汇总\n")
        f.write(f"时间范围: 2026-01-01 ~ 2026-01-31\n")
        f.write(f"下载时间: {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')}\n\n")
        f.write(f"知识库文档: {success} 个\n")

        f.write("妙记视频需在飞书客户端中打开链接后点击下载\n")
    
    print("\n" + "=" * 50)
    print(f"✅ 完成！文件已保存到 {OUTPUT_DIR}")
    print("=" * 50)
    print("\n⚠️ 妙记视频需手动下载：打开妙记链接后点击【下载】按钮")

    """递归列出云空间文件"""
    if all_files is None:
        all_files = []
    
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}
    
    # 飞书 drive explorer API
    url = f"https://open.feishu.cn/open-apis/drive/explorer/v2/folder/{folder_token}/children"
    params = {"page_size": 200}

    data = r.json()
    
    if data.get("code") != 0:
        print(f"❌ 列出文件夹失败: {data.get('msg')}")
        return all_files
    
    items = data.get("data", {}).get("entities", [])
    
    for item in items:
        obj = item.get("obj", {})
        name = obj.get("name", "未命名")
        obj_token = obj.get("token", "")
        obj_type = obj.get("type", "")  # doc, docx, sheet, minute, folder 等
        created_time = parse_time(obj.get("create_time", 0))
        modified_time = parse_time(obj.get("edit_time", 0))
        
        full_path = f"{path}{name}"
        
        if obj_type == "folder":
            list_drive_files(token, obj_token, all_files, f"{full_path}/")
        else:
            all_files.append({
                "name": name,
                "token": obj_token,
                "type": obj_type,
                "path": full_path,
                "created_time": created_time,
                "modified_time": modified_time,
            })
    
    return all_files
  new_string: def list_drive_files(token, folder_token, all_files=None, path=""):
    """递归列出云空间文件（drive v1 files API）"""
    if all_files is None:
        all_files = []
    
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}
    
    # 飞书 drive v1 files API
    url = "https://open.feishu.cn/open-apis/drive/v1/files"
    params = {"folder_token": folder_token, "page_size": 200}
    page_token = None
    
    while True:
        if page_token:
            params["page_token"] = page_token
        r = requests.get(url, headers=headers, params=params, timeout=30)
        data = r.json()
        
        if data.get("code") != 0:
            print(f"❌ 列出文件夹失败: {data.get('msg')}")
            return all_files
        
        files = data.get("data", {}).get("files", [])
        
        for f in files:
            name = f.get("name", "未命名")
            obj_token = f.get("token", "")
            obj_type = f.get("type", "docx")  # doc, docx, sheet, folder, minute 等
            created_time = parse_time(f.get("create_time", f.get("created_time", 0)))
            modified_time = parse_time(f.get("edit_time", f.get("modified_time", 0)))
            full_path = f"{path}{name}"
            
            if obj_type == "folder":
                list_drive_files(token, obj_token, all_files, f"{full_path}/")
            else:
                all_files.append({
                    "name": name,
                    "token": obj_token,
                    "type": obj_type,
                    "path": full_path,
                    "created_time": created_time,
                    "modified_time": modified_time,
                })
        
        page_token = data.get("data", {}).get("next_page_token")
        if not page_token:
            break
    
    return all_files

  old_string: def parse_time(ts):
    """解析时间戳（支持秒和毫秒）"""
    if not ts:
        return 0
    t = int(ts)
    if t > 10000000000:
        t = t // 1000
    return t
  new_string: def parse_time(ts):
    """解析时间戳（支持秒、毫秒、ISO格式）"""
    if not ts:
        return 0
    if isinstance(ts, str):
        try:
            dt = datetime.fromisoformat(ts.replace("Z", "+00:00"))
            return int(dt.timestamp())
        except:
            return int(ts) if ts.isdigit() else 0
    t = int(ts)
    if t > 10000000000:
        t = t // 1000
    return t

  new_string: def _parse_file_item(item, path=""):
    """解析单个文件/文件夹项（兼容 drive v1 和 explorer v2 格式）"""
    name = item.get("name", item.get("title", "未命名"))
    obj_token = item.get("token", item.get("file_token", ""))
    obj_type = item.get("type", item.get("obj_type", "docx"))

        "token": obj_token,
        "type": obj_type,
        "path": f"{path}{name}",
        "created_time": created_time,
        "modified_time": modified_time,
    }


def list_drive_files(token, folder_token, all_files=None, path=""):
    """递归列出云空间文件（优先 drive explorer v2，回退 drive v1）"""
    if all_files is None:
        all_files = []
    
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}
    
    # 优先尝试 drive explorer v2 API
    url_v2 = f"https://open.feishu.cn/open-apis/drive/explorer/v2/items/{folder_token}/children"
    params_v2 = {"page_size": 200}
    page_token = None
    api_used = "explorer_v2"
    
    while True:
        if page_token:
            params_v2["page_token"] = page_token
        try:
            r = requests.get(url_v2, headers=headers, params=params_v2, timeout=30)
            r.raise_for_status()
            data = r.json()
        except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
            print(f"   ⚠️ Explorer v2 请求失败: {e}")
            break
        except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
            print(f"   ⚠️ Explorer v2 响应非JSON: {e}")
            break
        
        if data.get("code") != 0:
            # 回退到 drive v1
            if api_used == "explorer_v2":
                api_used = "drive_v1"
                page_token = None
                url_v1 = "https://open.feishu.cn/open-apis/drive/v1/files"
                params_v1 = {"folder_token": folder_token, "page_size": 200}
                continue
            else:
                print(f"❌ 列出文件夹失败: {data.get('msg', data)}")
                return all_files
        
        # 解析响应（explorer v2 用 items，drive v1 用 files）
        items = data.get("data", {}).get("items", data.get("data", {}).get("files", []))
        
        for item in items:
            parsed = _parse_file_item(item, path)
            if parsed["type"] == "folder":
                list_drive_files(token, parsed["token"], all_files, f"{parsed['path']}/")
            else:
                all_files.append(parsed)
        
        page_token = data.get("data", {}).get("page_token", data.get("data", {}).get("next_page_token"))
        if not page_token:
            break
        time.sleep(0.2)  # 避免请求过快
    
    return all_files

        time.sleep(0.2)  # 避免请求过快
    
    return all_files
  new_string: def _fetch_page(token, folder_token, path, page_token, use_v1=False):
    """获取一页文件列表，返回 (items, next_page_token, error_msg)"""
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}
    if use_v1:
        url = "https://open.feishu.cn/open-apis/drive/v1/files"
        params = {"folder_token": folder_token, "page_size": 200}
        if page_token:
            params["page_token"] = page_token
    else:
        url = f"https://open.feishu.cn/open-apis/drive/explorer/v2/items/{folder_token}/children"
        params = {"page_size": 200}
        if page_token:
            params["page_token"] = page_token
    try:
        r = requests.get(url, headers=headers, params=params, timeout=30)
        r.raise_for_status()
        data = r.json()
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        return [], None, str(e)
    except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
        return [], None, f"响应非JSON: {e}"
    if data.get("code") != 0:
        return [], None, data.get("msg", str(data))
    d = data.get("data", {})
    items = d.get("items", d.get("files", []))
    next_token = d.get("page_token") or d.get("next_page_token")
    return items, next_token, None


def list_drive_files(token, folder_token, all_files=None, path=""):
    """递归列出云空间文件（优先 drive explorer v2，回退 drive v1）"""
    if all_files is None:
        all_files = []
    
    page_token = None
    use_v1 = False
    
    while True:
        items, next_token, err = _fetch_page(token, folder_token, path, page_token, use_v1)
        if err:
            if not use_v1:
                print(f"   ⚠️ Explorer v2 失败，尝试 drive v1: {err}")
                use_v1 = True
                page_token = None
                continue
            print(f"❌ 列出文件夹失败: {err}")
            return all_files
        
        for item in items:
            parsed = _parse_file_item(item, path)
            if parsed["type"] == "folder":
                list_drive_files(token, parsed["token"], all_files, f"{parsed['path']}/")
            else:
                all_files.append(parsed)
        
        if not next_token:
            break
        page_token = next_token
        time.sleep(0.2)
    
    return all_files

def list_minutes_january(user_token):
    """列出1月妙记（使用tenant_token）"""
    token = get_tenant_token()
    if not token:
        print("   ⚠️ 无法获取应用Token，跳过妙记列表")
        return []
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}
    url = "https://open.feishu.cn/open-apis/minutes/v1/minutes"
    params = {"page_size": 50, "start_time": str(START_TS), "end_time": str(END_TS)}
    try:
        r = requests.get(url, headers=headers, params=params, timeout=30)
        data = r.json()
        if data.get("code") == 0:
            return data.get("data", {}).get("items", [])
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"   ⚠️ 妙记API异常: {e}")
    return []
  new_string: def get_tenant_token():
    """获取应用tenant_token（妙记API需要，可选）"""
    APP_ID = "cli_a48818290ef8100d"
    APP_SECRET = "dhjU0qWd5AzicGWTf4cTqhCWJOrnuCk4"
    url = "https://open.feishu.cn/open-apis/auth/v3/tenant_access_token/internal"
    try:
        r = requests.post(url, json={"app_id": APP_ID, "app_secret": APP_SECRET}, timeout=10)
        data = r.json()
        return data.get("tenant_access_token") if data.get("code") == 0 else None
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"   ⚠️ 获取应用Token失败: {e}")
        return None


def list_minutes_from_api():
    """通过妙记API列出1月妙记（需 minutes 权限，可能不可用）"""
    token = get_tenant_token()
    if not token:
        return []
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}
    url = "https://open.feishu.cn/open-apis/minutes/v1/minutes"
    params = {"page_size": 50, "start_time": str(START_TS), "end_time": str(END_TS)}
    try:
        r = requests.get(url, headers=headers, params=params, timeout=30)
        data = r.json()
        if data.get("code") == 0:
            return data.get("data", {}).get("items", [])
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"   ⚠️ 妙记API异常: {e}")
    return []


def minutes_from_drive_files(files):
    """从云空间文件列表中提取妙记（type=minute）"""
    return [f for f in files if f.get("type") == "minute" or f.get("type") == "minute_file"]

  old_string: def parse_time(ts):
    """解析时间戳（支持秒、毫秒、ISO格式）"""
    if not ts:
        return 0
    if isinstance(ts, str):
        try:
            dt = datetime.fromisoformat(ts.replace("Z", "+00:00"))
            return int(dt.timestamp())
        except:
            return int(ts) if ts.isdigit() else 0
    t = int(ts)
    if t > 10000000000:
        t = t // 1000
    return t
  new_string: def parse_time(ts):
    """解析时间戳（支持秒、毫秒、ISO格式）"""
    if ts is None or ts == "":
        return 0
    if isinstance(ts, str):
        try:
            dt = datetime.fromisoformat(ts.replace("Z", "+00:00").split(".")[0])
            return int(dt.timestamp())
        except Exception:
            pass
        if ts.isdigit():
            t = int(ts)
            if t > 10000000000:
                t = t // 1000
            return t
        return 0
    try:
        t = int(ts)
        if t > 10000000000:
            t = t // 1000
        return t
    except (TypeError, ValueError):
        return 0

  old_string: def list_minutes_from_api():
    """通过妙记API列出1月妙记（需 minutes 权限，可能不可用）"""
    token = get_tenant_token()
    if not token:
        return []
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}
    url = "https://open.feishu.cn/open-apis/minutes/v1/minutes"
    params = {"page_size": 50, "start_time": str(START_TS), "end_time": str(END_TS)}
    try:
        r = requests.get(url, headers=headers, params=params, timeout=30)
        data = r.json()
        if data.get("code") == 0:
            return data.get("data", {}).get("items", [])
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"   ⚠️ 妙记API异常: {e}")
    return []
  new_string: def list_minutes_from_api():
    """通过妙记API列出1月妙记（需 minutes 权限，可能不可用）"""
    token = get_tenant_token()
    if not token:
        return []
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}
    url = "https://open.feishu.cn/open-apis/minutes/v1/minutes"
    params = {"page_size": 50, "start_time": str(START_TS), "end_time": str(END_TS)}
    try:
        r = requests.get(url, headers=headers, params=params, timeout=30)
        text = r.text
        if not text or not text.strip().startswith("{"):
            return []
        data = json.loads(text)
        if data.get("code") == 0:
            return data.get("data", {}).get("items", [])
    except json.JSONDecodeError:
        pass  # API可能返回非JSON（如HTML错误页）
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"   ⚠️ 妙记API异常: {e}")
    return []

### 1. Drive API
- **Explorer v2** 返回 404，已改为优先使用 **drive v1** 并自动回退

- 增加 JSON 解析异常处理

- `get_tenant_token` 不再依赖 `.feishu_tokens.json`，直接使用应用凭证
- 妙记优先从云空间文件（`type=minute`）提取，其次尝试妙记 API
- 妙记 API 若返回非 JSON，会静默跳过，不再报错

### 4. 时间解析与兜底
- 改进 `parse_time`，支持秒、毫秒、ISO 字符串
- 若无法解析创建时间，则处理该文件夹下的全部文件

### 5. 命令行参数
- `--folder` / `-f`：云空间文件夹 token
- `--output` / `-o`：保存目录

  command: cd /Users/karuo/Documents/个人/卡若AI && python3 << 'PYEOF'
import os
import re
from pathlib import Path

# 1月聊天记录文件
base = Path("/Users/karuo/Documents/聊天记录")
jan_files = [
    base / "soul 派对84场 20260127.txt",
    base / "soul/soul 创业派对。85场 20260128.txt",
    base / "soul/soul 派对 86场 20260129 .txt",
    base / "Soul 团队会议 39场 20260129 卡若.txt",
    base / "产研团队 第21场 20260129 许永平.txt",
    base / "soul 派对 88场 20260131.txt",
    base / "流光1月28日.txt",
    base / "soul/soul 派对 87场 20260130.txt",
]

# 提取说话人/角色名
names = set()
for f in jan_files:
    if not f.exists():
        continue
    t = f.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore")
    # 说话人 X / 角色名 格式
    for m in re.finditer(r"(?:说话人|卡若|芷萍|南风|许永平|±极|韩阳|刘光|刘硕|阿猫|婼瑄|梦雨|船长|玉斌|小花|彩燕|游威|潘宁|顾离|海萍)[^\s]*", t):
        names.add(m.group(0).strip())
    for m in re.finditer(r"([^\s]{2,4})(?:老师|总|老板|哥|姐)\s", t):
        names.add(m.group(1) + "老师" if "老师" in m.group(0) else m.group(1))
    for m in re.finditer(r"(\w{2,4})\s+\d+:\d+", t):
        n = m.group(1)
        if len(n) >= 2 and n not in ("说话人", "文字", "关键词"):
            names.add(n)

# 输出人名
for n in sorted(names):
    if re.match(r"^[\u4e00-\u9fa5a-zA-Z]{2,6}$", n):
        print(n)
PYEOF

  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/个人/卡若AI/02_卡人（水）/_团队成员/水桥/飞书管理/scripts/write_renmai_to_feishu.py
  contents: #!/usr/bin/env python3
"""写入人脉到飞书【卡若日志-2月】火4、人脉块"""
import os
import sys
import json
import requests

SCRIPT_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))
sys.path.insert(0, SCRIPT_DIR)
from auto_log import get_token_silent, get_wiki_token

# 1月提取人脉（简洁名）
RENMAI = [
    ("知己/MBTI", ["韩阳", "刘光", "刘硕", "婼瑄", "大大", "梦雨", "玉斌", "小诺", "船长"]),
    ("产研/技术", ["许永平", "芷萍", "南风", "游威", "潘宁", "海萍"]),
    ("Soul/外部", ["小花", "顾离"]),
]

def main():
    token = get_token_silent()
    if not token:
        print("❌ 无法获取Token")
        sys.exit(1)
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}
    wiki_token = get_wiki_token()
    r = requests.get(
        f"https://open.feishu.cn/open-apis/wiki/v2/spaces/get_node?token={wiki_token}",
        headers=headers, timeout=30
    )
    if r.json().get("code") != 0:
        print("❌ 获取文档失败")
        sys.exit(1)
    doc_id = r.json()["data"]["node"]["obj_token"]
    r = requests.get(
        f"https://open.feishu.cn/open-apis/docx/v1/documents/{doc_id}/blocks",
        headers=headers, params={"page_size": 500}, timeout=30
    )
    blocks = r.json().get("data", {}).get("items", [])
    renmai_block_id = None
    for b in blocks:
        h = b.get("heading3", {})
        for el in h.get("elements", []):
            c = el.get("text_run", {}).get("content", "")
            if "人脉" in c:
                renmai_block_id = b.get("block_id")
                break
        if renmai_block_id:
            break
    if not renmai_block_id:
        print("❌ 未找到「人脉」块")
        sys.exit(1)
    children = []
    for label, names in RENMAI:
        children.append({
            "block_type": 2,
            "text": {"elements": [{"text_run": {"content": f"{label}：{''.join(names)}", "text_element_style": {}}}], "style": {}}
        })
    r = requests.post(
        f"https://open.feishu.cn/open-apis/docx/v1/documents/{doc_id}/blocks/{renmai_block_id}/children",
        headers=headers, json={"children": children, "index": 0}, timeout=30
    )
    if r.json().get("code") == 0:
        print("✅ 人脉已写入飞书【卡若日志-2月】火4、人脉块")
    else:
        print(f"❌ 写入失败: {r.json().get('msg')}")
        sys.exit(1)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

import os
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime

# 1月1日-31日时间戳
START = int(datetime(2026, 1, 1).timestamp())
END = int(datetime(2026, 1, 31, 23, 59, 59).timestamp())

# 搜索范围：个人、卡若AI、聊天记录
roots = [
    Path("/Users/karuo/Documents/个人"),
    Path("/Users/karuo/Documents/聊天记录"),
]
# 排除目录
skip = {".git", "node_modules", "__pycache__", ".cursor", ".DS_Store"}

files = []
for root in roots:
    if not root.exists():
        continue
    for p in root.rglob("*"):
        if p.is_dir() or any(s in str(p) for s in skip):
            continue
        try:
            st = p.stat()
            # macOS: st_birthtime 创建, st_mtime 修改
            ct = int(getattr(st, "st_birthtime", st.st_mtime))
            mt = int(st.st_mtime)
            if START <= ct <= END or START <= mt <= END:
                files.append((str(p), ct, mt))
        except:
            pass

# 按修改时间排序
files.sort(key=lambda x: x[2], reverse=True)
for f, ct, mt in files[:80]:
    print(f"{datetime.fromtimestamp(mt).strftime('%Y-%m-%d')} | {f}")
print(f"\n共 {len(files)} 个1月文件")

from datetime import datetime

exts = {".txt", ".md", ".json"}

<mcp_instructions description="Instructions provided by MCP servers to help use them properly">
Server: cursor-ide-browser
The cursor-ide-browser is an MCP server that allows you to navigate the web and interact with the page. Use this for frontend/webapp development and testing code changes.

CRITICAL - Lock/unlock workflow:
1. browser_lock requires an existing browser tab - you CANNOT lock before browser_navigate
2. Correct order: browser_navigate -> browser_lock -> (interactions) -> browser_unlock
3. If a browser tab already exists (check with browser_tabs list), call browser_lock FIRST before any interactions
4. Only call browser_unlock when completely done with ALL browser operations for this turn

IMPORTANT - Before interacting with any page:
1. Use browser_tabs with action "list" to see open tabs and their URLs
2. Use browser_snapshot to get the page structure and element refs before any interaction (click, type, hover, etc.)

IMPORTANT - Waiting strategy:
When waiting for page changes (navigation, content loading, animations, etc.), prefer short incremental waits (1-3 seconds) with browser_snapshot checks in between rather than a single long wait. For example, instead of waiting 10 seconds, do: wait 2s -> snapshot -> check if ready -> if not, wait 2s more -> snapshot again. This allows you to proceed as soon as the page is ready rather than always waiting the maximum time.

Notes:
- Native dialogs (alert/confirm/prompt) never block automation. By default, confirm() returns true and prompt() returns the default value. To test different responses, call browser_handle_dialog BEFORE the triggering action: use accept: false for "Cancel", or promptText: "value" for custom prompt input.
- Iframe content is not accessible - only elements outside iframes can be interacted with.
- Use browser_type to append text, browser_fill to clear and replace. browser_fill also works on contenteditable elements.
- For nested scroll containers, use browser_scroll with scrollIntoView: true before clicking elements that may be obscured.
</mcp_instructions>

  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/个人/卡若AI/02_卡人（水）/_团队成员/水桥/飞书管理/scripts/read_feishu_renmai.py
  contents: #!/usr/bin/env python3
"""读取飞书1月/2月文档的「人脉」块内容，用于验证写入"""
import sys
sys.path.insert(0, __file__.rsplit("/", 1)[0])
from auto_log import get_token_silent

WIKI_TOKENS = {
    1: ("JZiiwxEjHiRxouk8hSPcqBn6nrd", "2026年1月 运营团队启动"),
    2: ("Jn2EwXP2OiTujNkAbNCcDcM7nRA", "2026年2月 突破执行"),
}

def get_doc_id(token, headers):
    import requests
    r = requests.get(
        f"https://open.feishu.cn/open-apis/wiki/v2/spaces/get_node?token={token}",
        headers=headers, timeout=30
    )
    if r.json().get("code") != 0:
        return None
    return r.json()["data"]["node"]["obj_token"]

def get_blocks(doc_id, headers, parent_id=None):
    import requests
    url = f"https://open.feishu.cn/open-apis/docx/v1/documents/{doc_id}/blocks"
    params = {"page_size": 500}
    if parent_id:
        params["parent_block_id"] = parent_id
    r = requests.get(url, headers=headers, params=params, timeout=30)
    data = r.json()
    if data.get("code") != 0:
        return []
    return data.get("data", {}).get("items", [])

def text_from_block(b):
    for k in ("text", "heading1", "heading2", "heading3", "paragraph"):
        v = b.get(k, {})
        if not v:
            continue
        for el in v.get("elements", []):
            c = el.get("text_run", {}).get("content", "")
            if c:
                return c.strip()
    return ""

def main():
    token = get_token_silent()
    if not token:
        print("❌ 无法获取Token")
        sys.exit(1)
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}

    for month, (wiki_token, label) in WIKI_TOKENS.items():
        print(f"\n{'='*50}")
        print(f"📄 {label} (token: {wiki_token[:12]}...)")
        print("="*50)
        doc_id = get_doc_id(wiki_token, headers)
        if not doc_id:
            print("  ❌ 获取文档失败")
            continue
        blocks = get_blocks(doc_id, headers)
        renmai_block_id = None
        for b in blocks:
            h = b.get("heading3", {})
            for el in h.get("elements", []):
                c = el.get("text_run", {}).get("content", "")
                if "人脉" in c:
                    renmai_block_id = b.get("block_id")
                    break
            if renmai_block_id:
                break
        if not renmai_block_id:
            print("  ⚠️ 未找到「人脉」块")
            continue
        children = get_blocks(doc_id, headers, parent_id=renmai_block_id)
        if not children:
            print("  ⚠️ 人脉块下无子内容（可能为空）")
        else:
            for i, c in enumerate(children, 1):
                t = text_from_block(c)
                if t:
                    print(f"  {i}. {t}")
    print("\n✅ 读取完成")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

"""写入人脉到飞书【卡若日志】火4、人脉块。支持 --month 1/2 指定目标文档"""
import argparse
import os
import sys
import json
import requests

SCRIPT_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))
sys.path.insert(0, SCRIPT_DIR)
from auto_log import get_token_silent, WIKI_TOKENS

# 1月提取人脉（简洁名）
RENMAI = [
    ("知己/MBTI", ["韩阳", "刘光", "刘硕", "婼瑄", "大大", "梦雨", "玉斌", "小诺", "船长"]),
    ("产研/技术", ["许永平", "芷萍", "南风", "游威", "潘宁", "海萍"]),
    ("Soul/外部", ["小花", "顾离"]),
]

def main():
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="写入人脉到飞书卡若日志")
    parser.add_argument("--month", type=int, default=None, help="目标月份 1 或 2，不指定则用当前月份")
    args = parser.parse_args()
    month = args.month
    if month is None:
        from datetime import datetime
        month = datetime.now().month
    wiki_token = WIKI_TOKENS.get(month, WIKI_TOKENS[1])
    labels = {1: "2026年1月 运营团队启动", 2: "2026年2月 突破执行"}
    target_label = labels.get(month, f"{month}月")

    token = get_token_silent()
    if not token:
        print("❌ 无法获取Token")
        sys.exit(1)
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}

## 问题与处理

1. **之前写入目标错误**：`write_renmai_to_feishu.py` 使用 `get_wiki_token()`，按当前月份选文档，2 月运行时写入的是 2 月文档，而不是 1 月。
2. **1 月文档结构不同**：1 月文档只有「金、本月最重要的任务」和日期条目，没有「人脉」块。

## 已做修改

1. **`read_feishu_renmai.py`**：新增脚本，用于读取并校验 1 月、2 月飞书文档的人脉块。
2. **`write_renmai_to_feishu.py`**：
   - 支持 `--month 1` / `--month 2` 指定目标文档；
   - 若目标文档无人脉块，会先创建「火 4、人脉」块再写入。

## 使用方式

```bash
# 写入 1 月文档
python3 write_renmai_to_feishu.py --month 1

# 写入 2 月文档
python3 write_renmai_to_feishu.py --month 2

# 验证 1 月、2 月人脉内容
python3 read_feishu_renmai.py
```
